fGqKFv"><div class="Box-sc-g0xbh4-0 eoaCFS js-snippet-clipboard-copy-unpositioned undefined" data-hpc="true"><article class="markdown-body entry-content container-lg" itemprop="text"><div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h1 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Configuring the SDK</h1><a id="user-content-configuring-the-sdk" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Configuring the SDK" href="#configuring-the-sdk"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">API keys and clients</h2><a id="user-content-api-keys-and-clients" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: API keys and clients" href="#api-keys-and-clients"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">By default, the SDK looks for the <code>OPENAI_API_KEY</code> environment variable for LLM requests and tracing, as soon as it is imported. If you are unable to set that environment variable before your app starts, you can use the [set_default_openai_key()][agents.set_default_openai_key] function to set the key.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="from agents import set_default_openai_key

set_default_openai_key(&quot;sk-...&quot;)"><pre><span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s1">agents</span> <span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-s1">set_default_openai_key</span>

<span class="pl-en">set_default_openai_key</span>(<span class="pl-s">"sk-..."</span>)</pre></div>
<p dir="auto">Alternatively, you can also configure an OpenAI client to be used. By default, the SDK creates an <code>AsyncOpenAI</code> instance, using the API key from the environment variable or the default key set above. You can change this by using the [set_default_openai_client()][agents.set_default_openai_client] function.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="from openai import AsyncOpenAI
from agents import set_default_openai_client

custom_client = AsyncOpenAI(base_url=&quot;...&quot;, api_key=&quot;...&quot;)
set_default_openai_client(custom_client)"><pre><span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s1">openai</span> <span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-v">AsyncOpenAI</span>
<span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s1">agents</span> <span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-s1">set_default_openai_client</span>

<span class="pl-s1">custom_client</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">AsyncOpenAI</span>(<span class="pl-s1">base_url</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">"..."</span>, <span class="pl-s1">api_key</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">"..."</span>)
<span class="pl-en">set_default_openai_client</span>(<span class="pl-s1">custom_client</span>)</pre></div>
<p dir="auto">Finally, you can also customize the OpenAI API that is used. By default, we use the OpenAI Responses API. You can override this to use the Chat Completions API by using the [set_default_openai_api()][agents.set_default_openai_api] function.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="from agents import set_default_openai_api

set_default_openai_api(&quot;chat_completions&quot;)"><pre><span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s1">agents</span> <span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-s1">set_default_openai_api</span>

<span class="pl-en">set_default_openai_api</span>(<span class="pl-s">"chat_completions"</span>)</pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Tracing</h2><a id="user-content-tracing" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Tracing" href="#tracing"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Tracing is enabled by default. It uses the OpenAI API keys from the section above by default (i.e. the environment variable or the default key you set). You can specifically set the API key used for tracing by using the [<code>set_tracing_export_api_key</code>][agents.set_tracing_export_api_key] function.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="from agents import set_tracing_export_api_key

set_tracing_export_api_key(&quot;sk-...&quot;)"><pre><span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s1">agents</span> <span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-s1">set_tracing_export_api_key</span>

<span class="pl-en">set_tracing_export_api_key</span>(<span class="pl-s">"sk-..."</span>)</pre></div>
<p dir="auto">You can also disable tracing entirely by using the [<code>set_tracing_disabled()</code>][agents.set_tracing_disabled] function.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="from agents import set_tracing_disabled

set_tracing_disabled(True)"><pre><span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s1">agents</span> <span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-s1">set_tracing_disabled</span>

<span class="pl-en">set_tracing_disabled</span>(<span class="pl-c1">True</span>)</pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Debug logging</h2><a id="user-content-debug-logging" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Debug logging" href="#debug-logging"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">The SDK has two Python loggers without any handlers set. By default, this means that warnings and errors are sent to <code>stdout</code>, but other logs are suppressed.</p>
<p dir="auto">To enable verbose logging, use the [<code>enable_verbose_stdout_logging()</code>][agents.enable_verbose_stdout_logging] function.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="from agents import enable_verbose_stdout_logging

enable_verbose_stdout_logging()"><pre><span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s1">agents</span> <span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-s1">enable_verbose_stdout_logging</span>

<span class="pl-en">enable_verbose_stdout_logging</span>()</pre></div>
<p dir="auto">Alternatively, you can customize the logs by adding handlers, filters, formatters, etc. You can read more in the <a href="https://docs.python.org/3/howto/logging.html" rel="nofollow">Python logging guide</a>.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="import logging

logger = logging.getLogger(&quot;openai.agents&quot;) # or openai.agents.tracing for the Tracing logger

# To make all logs show up
logger.setLevel(logging.DEBUG)
# To make info and above show up
logger.setLevel(logging.INFO)
# To make warning and above show up
logger.setLevel(logging.WARNING)
# etc

# You can customize this as needed, but this will output to `stderr` by default
logger.addHandler(logging.StreamHandler())"><pre><span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-s1">logging</span>

<span class="pl-s1">logger</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">logging</span>.<span class="pl-c1">getLogger</span>(<span class="pl-s">"openai.agents"</span>) <span class="pl-c"># or openai.agents.tracing for the Tracing logger</span>

<span class="pl-c"># To make all logs show up</span>
<span class="pl-s1">logger</span>.<span class="pl-c1">setLevel</span>(<span class="pl-s1">logging</span>.<span class="pl-c1">DEBUG</span>)
<span class="pl-c"># To make info and above show up</span>
<span class="pl-s1">logger</span>.<span class="pl-c1">setLevel</span>(<span class="pl-s1">logging</span>.<span class="pl-c1">INFO</span>)
<span class="pl-c"># To make warning and above show up</span>
<span class="pl-s1">logger</span>.<span class="pl-c1">setLevel</span>(<span class="pl-s1">logging</span>.<span class="pl-c1">WARNING</span>)
<span class="pl-c"># etc</span>

<span class="pl-c"># You can customize this as needed, but this will output to `stderr` by default</span>
<span class="pl-s1">logger</span>.<span class="pl-c1">addHandler</span>(<span class="pl-s1">logging</span>.<span class="pl-c1">StreamHandler</span>())</pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Sensitive data in logs</h3><a id="user-content-sensitive-data-in-logs" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Sensitive data in logs" href="#sensitive-data-in-logs"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Certain logs may contain sensitive data (for example, user data). If you want to disable this data from being logged, set the following environment variables.</p>
<p dir="auto">To disable logging LLM inputs and outputs:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="export OPENAI_AGENTS_DONT_LOG_MODEL_DATA=1"><pre><span class="pl-k">export</span> OPENAI_AGENTS_DONT_LOG_MODEL_DATA=1</pre></div>
<p dir="auto">To disable logging tool inputs and outputs:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="export OPENAI_AGENTS_DONT_LOG_TOOL_DATA=1"><pre><span class="pl-k">export</span> OPENAI_AGENTS_DONT_LOG_TOOL_DATA=1</pre></div>
